Back to matrix

yaml-test-suite Framework Matrix - Test 2XXW

Spec Example 2.25. Unordered Sets

YAML

# Sets are represented as a
# Mapping where each key is
# associated with a null value
--- !!set
? Mark McGwire
? Sammy Sosa
? Ken Griff

Expected Events

+STR
+DOC ---
+MAP <tag:yaml.org,2002:set>
=VAL :Mark McGwire
=VAL :
=VAL :Sammy Sosa
=VAL :
=VAL :Ken Griff
=VAL :
-MAP
-DOC
-STR

Expected JSON

]

  "Sammy Sosa": null,
  "Ken Griff": null
}
